    ->     e.id,

    ->     CASE 
    ->         WHEN ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY e.id ORDER BY e.id) <= e.total_seats * 0.3 THEN 'VIP'
    ->         WHEN ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY e.id ORDER BY e.id) <= e.total_seats * 0.7 THEN 'Premium'
    ->         ELSE 'Standard'
    ->     END as section

    ->     SELECT a.N + b.N * 10 + c.N * 100 + d.N * 1000 + 1 as seat_num

mysql> INSERT INTO seats (event_id, seat_number, row_name, section)
    -> SELECT 
    ->     event_id,
    ->     LPAD(row_num, 3, '0') AS seat_number,
    ->     CHAR(65 + FLOOR((row_num - 1) / 20)) AS row_name,
    ->     CASE 
    ->         WHEN row_num <= total_seats * 0.3 THEN 'VIP'
    ->         WHEN row_num <= total_seats * 0.7 THEN 'Premium'
    ->         ELSE 'Standard'
    ->     END AS section
    -> FROM (
    ->     SELECT
    ->         e.id AS event_id,
    ->         e.total_seats,
    ->         ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY e.id ORDER BY numbers.seat_num) AS row_num
    ->     FROM events e
    ->     JOIN (
    ->         SELECT a.N + b.N * 10 + c.N * 100 + d.N * 1000 + 1 AS seat_num
    ->         FROM (SELECT 0 AS N UNION SELECT 1 UNION SELECT 2 UNION SELECT 3 UNION SELECT 4

mysql> CREATE TABLE seats (
    ->     id INT PRIMARY KEY AUTO_INCREMENT,
    ->     event_id INT NOT NULL,
    ->     seat_number VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    ->     row_name VARCHAR(5) NOT NULL,
    ->     section VARCHAR(20),
    ->     is_booked BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    ->     booking_id INT NULL,
    ->     created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    -> 
    ->     -- Foreign Keys
    ->     FOREIGN KEY (event_id) REFERENCES events(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    ->     FOREIGN KEY (booking_id) REFERENCES bookings(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    -> 
    ->     -- Unique constraint to prevent duplicate seats per event
    ->     UNIQUE KEY unique_seat_per_event (event_id, seat_number, row_name)
    -> );

mysql> INSERT INTO seats (event_id, seat_number, row_name, section)
    -> SELECT 
    ->     e.id AS event_id,

    ->     CHAR(65 + FLOOR((numbers.n - 1) / 20)) AS row_name,

    ->         WHEN numbers.n <= e.total_seats * 0.7 THEN 'Premium'
    ->         ELSE 'Standard'

    -> FROM events e
